msg:Pros: location, modern facilities, COVID test organization, assistance from staff, turn down service included a Snickers, free health kit upon check in, spacious bathtubs, free orange juice daily, a robot that will deliver your outdoor food orders, complimentary upgrade to an all female floor and panoramic room

Cons: breakfast (It was honestly shocking how poor the breakfast was for a 5 star restaurant. Very limited options and only a few of each things were available. Might be because of COVID restrictions but I never left feeling full or pleased after eating)

I'd definitely suggest this hotel if you want to stay in the French quarter and also want to go to Disney. Disney is at the end of line 11 and Hongqiao airport is on the end of line 10 (both walking distance from the hotel). But perhaps don't pay extra for the breakfast and instead enjoy some meals at a nearby restaurant.

msg:Because of the pleasant experience of staying and dining before, I did not hesitate to choose Xingguo Hotel on New Year's Day, and returned with satisfaction. After several stays, I finally wrote a review.
 The villas of Xingguo Hotel were first developed by Swire Pacific. Its No. 1 building is a luxurious headquarters building and Taipan residence.
Xingguo Hotel No. 1 is a two-story brick-concrete structure built in 1934, known as the "little white house". It was the Taipan residence of the British businessman Taikoo Foreign Company. It was the office of the Municipal Party Committee after the founding of New China. It was the Xingguo Guest House that hosted Chairman Mao, Premier Zhou and other central leaders. Unfortunately, if the housing is not full, Building One will not be open, unfortunately.
        The hotel is elegant and elegant, the staff can smile, and it is very comfortable to lie down by the pool... Happy hour provides ice cream! This~ alright. Little sister, it's delicious too.

Xingguo Hotel Features:
The only big garden in Shanghai with 70,000 square meters in the city center,
The only hotel in Shanghai was rated as the first truly green hotel in Shanghai, and the only whole 16th floor in Shanghai is a complete set of presidential suites.
The only Clark International Chain Fitness Center in Shanghai that has the only transparent zenith and garden view in Shanghai (this one is old)
The only international brand business hotel in China that has evolved from a state guesthouse to participate in international competition (that‚Äôs not the case, Ruijin has cooperated with InterContinental)
